online use-cases like mobile recharges, utility bill payments, travel, movies, and events bookings as well as in-store payments at grocery stores, fruits and vegetable shops, restaurants, parking, later added data card, postpaid mobile and landline bill payments in 2013.", "[10]\n By January 2014, the company launched the Paytm Wallet, and the Indian Railways and Uber added it as a payment
